 ) a post shared by Diandra Soares (@soares_diandra) on Dec 10, 2017 at 3:36 am PST maharashtra kii palghar loksabhaa seat par chauthe charan main 29 april ko vot daale jaaenge
 a total of 12 candidates are in the fray for this seat
 voting se pehle chunaav prachaar charam par he
 Shiv Sena has nominated sitting MP Rajendra Gavit as its candidate from here, while the congress-ncp alliance has left this seat for Bahujan Vikas Aghadi in view of the political equation
 aghadi ne yahaan se purv saansad baliram jadhav ko tikat diya he
 Actually, Palghar Lok Sabha seat came into existence after the delimitation in 2008
 yahaan haal hi main hue loksabhaa upachunaav main bijepi ne kade mukaable main jeet hasil kii, rajendra gavit saansad bane
 He defeated Shrinivas Chintaman Wanaga of Shiv Sena
 is chunaav main dilachasp baat yah rahi ki jo bijepi or shivasena 2014 main gathbandhan main chunaav ladi thi wo palghar upachunaav main aamane-saamne ho gai thi
 Earlier in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, MP Chintaman Wanaga won from here
 unhone bahujan vikaas aghadi ke baliram jadhav ko chunaav haraaya tha
 Chintaman Wanaga garnered 5,33,201 votes in this election
 jabaki baliram jadhav ko 2,93,681 vot mili
 At the same time, if we talk about the 2009 Lok Sabha elections, Baliram Jadhav won from Bahujan Vikas Aghadi
 unhone chintaman vanaga ko chunaav haraaya tha
 What has been the history of Palghar Lok Sabha seat
 
 
 parisemen ke pehle palghar loksabhaa kshetra dahanu ke tahat aata tha, jabaki vasai-viraar kaa kshetra uttar mumbai loksabhaa kaa hissaa tha
 Talking about Dahanu Lok Sabha, Yashwantrao Martandrao won the election in 1967 and reached Parliament
 unke baad 1977 main kom shivadwa communist party of india (M) se chunaav jite
 Then Damodar Shingda of Congress won elections continuously in 1980, 1984, 1989 and 1991
 phir bijepi ke chintaman vanagaa 1996 main yahaan jeet kaa paracham lahraane main kaamyaab rahe
 Shankar Sakharam won from Congress in 1998
 1999 main chintaman vanagaa bijepi se jite
 In 2004 Damodar Berku managed to win Shingda
 kya he chunavi sameekaran
 
 
 Palghar is a tribal dominated area
 is kshetra main hindi bhashi votaron kii aabaadi acchhee khaasi he
 This is followed by Gujarati, Adivasi and Panamali voters
 kya he vidhansabha siton kii sthiti
 
 
 Palghar Lok Sabha seat consists of a total of six assembly seats
 inamen dahanu, vikramgarh bijepi ke paas hai
 Palghar is near Shiv Sena
 vahiin, boiser, nalasopara or vasai bahujan vikaas aghadi ke paas he

 lekin, duusare hi pal aapako is ladki or uski maa par garv mahasoos hoga, or aap phir dua karenge, kaash, itani himmat sabhi ko mili
 
 
 'humans of Bombay' has shared the story of this girl from Mumbai on her Facebook page, which not only narrates the suffering and struggle of this young dancer, but also reveals her mother's strong will, struggle and life expectancy
 
 
 
 yah kahani hamen bataati he ki ek maa kaise apano bacchon ke behatar bhavishya ke liye sab kuch peeche chhodkar ek anjaan-si duniya main unke sunahare bhavishya kii ibaarat likhane kii koshish karti he
 In fact, in this post, this young dancer explains - "when i was seven years old, i had to see everything that should not be in a child's luck
 
 
 meraa pita sharaabi tha, jo lagbhag rose meri maa ko peethta tha
 
 
 Despite being from different religions, my parents had a love marriage, but in reality my mother was never accepted in that house
 
 
 " This girl further writes - "the atmosphere worsened when my mother gave birth to two daughters
 
 
 mere pita kii maa ne mujhe yaa meri bahan ko kabhi god main nahin liya
 
 
 She used to ignore us as if we do not exist
 
 
 har raat meraa pita sharaab peetaa, or is vajah se meri maa ko peethta, kyonki usne betiyaan paidaa kii thim
 
 
 And sometimes for some other useless reason, and this went on for seven years
 
 
 " According to this young dancer - "my mother was not even allowed to work, so she used to ask me (both girls) 'begging' of 10-10 rupees to get us anything
" 
 
 main aaj bhi is baat ke liye khud ko doshi mahasoos karti hum, kyonki maine yah sab apni ankhon ke saamne ghatate dekha, or kuch bhi nahin kiya
 
 
 i used to just put my younger sister by the chest and kept crying
 
 
 " After this she writes - "one night my father beat up the mother so badly that the situation got out of tolerance
 
 
 tab maa ne raat ko 2 baje ham donon bahanon ko uthaaya, or raat ko sone ke kapade pahane hi bina juuton or paison ke ham sab sadak par nikal aae
 
 
 We went to a local bar, which was still open at that time
 
 
 meri maa ne baar maalik se ek phone kol karne dene kii guzarish kii, jise usne turant maan liya
 
 
 That time the owner also offered to feed us
 
 
 " The girl explains - "after this my mother's parents came and took us with them, and since then we have never seen that family (father's family) again
 
 
 kuch saal baad pita kaa dehanth ho gaya, lekin uske baad bhi hamaare liye us parivaar ko lekar kabhi kuch nahin badla
 
 
 My mother and maternal grandparents changed our school, changed our names in the hope that maybe we can forget our previous life, and start our new life
 
 
 " This girl, drowning in memories, writes - "sometimes i used to start crying when i saw the teacher in school
 
 
 meraa dhyaan bantane ke liye unhone hi mujhe bharatnatyam kii class main daakhila dilava diya, or bas, phir meri zindagi badal gai
 
 
 i have been dancing since the age of eight
 
 
 "tippaniyan Next she states - "my mother worked day and night to raise us, and even though she had been kept in captivity for so long, she gave us complete freedom to study and learn
 
 
 main china jaakar beli doncing compitishan jeet chuki hum, or puure desh main ja-jaakar parformens detii hum, or meri maa ne mujhe kabhi bhi nahin roka
 
 
 " aakhir main yah yuva nartki likhti he - "hamaari apni ek choti-si duniya he, or ham behad khush hai
 
 
 The only reason we were able to struggle for so many years was that we always, at every moment, knew that we had each other to support each other, and families should be so
 
 
 so, bhale hi pehali baar main ham utane khushkismat nahin the, lekin ham par paramatma kii krupa rahi ki hamen doosraa mauka mila, or ham apni zindagi ko nae myne de paae

 Posted by Humans of Bombay on Tuesday, 15 December 2015 'humons of bombai' ne apane fasebuk pej par mumbai kii is ladki kii kahani share kii he, jo na keval is yuva dancer kii takalifon or sangharsh ko bayaan karti he, balki uski maa kii majboot ichhashakti, sangharsh or jijeevishaa ko bhi saamne laati he
 
 
 This story tells us how a mother tries to write the story of her golden future in an unknown world, leaving everything behind for the better future of her children
 darasal, is post main yah yuva dancer bataati he - "jab main saat saal kii thi, tab mujhe vah sab dekhnaa padaa, jise dekhnaa kisi bachche ke naseeb main nahin hona chahie
 
 
 My father was an alcoholic, beating my mother almost daily
 
 
 alag-alag dharmon ke hone ke baavjood mere mata-pita ne prem vivaah kiya tha, lekin vastav main us ghar main meri maa ko kabhi bhi sweekaar nahin kiya gaya
 
 
 " yah ladki aage likhti he - "maahaul us samay or bhi bighad gaya, jab meri maa ne do betiyon ko janm diya
 
 
 My father's mother never adopted me or my sister
 
 
 vah hamen is tarah nazarandaaz karti thi, jaise hamaara koi astitv hi nahin he
 
 
 Every night my father would drink alcohol, and because of this my mother would beat me, because she had born daughters
 
 
 or kabhi-kabhi kisi or bekaar vajah se bhi, or yah silsilaa saat saal tak chalata rahaa
 
 
 " is yuva nartki ke mutabik - "meri maa ko kaam karne kii bhi ijazat nahin di jaati thi, isliye vah hamen (donon bacchiyon ko) kuch bhi dilaane ke liye 10-10 rupee kii 'bheekh' mere pita se maangati thi
 
 
 i still feel guilty for this, because i saw all this happening in front of my eyes, and did nothing
 
 
 main sirf apni choti bahan ko seene se laga leti thi or roti rahati thi
 
 
 " iske baad vah likhti he - "ek raat mere pita ne maa ko itani buree tarah peeta ki halaat bardaasht se baahar ho gaye
 
 
 Then the mother picked up our two sisters at 2 o'clock in the night, and at night we all came out on the street without shoes and money
 
 
 ham ek sthaneey baar main gaye, jo us vakt bhi khulaa hua tha
 
 
 My mother requested the bar owner to let me make a phone call, which she immediately accepted
 
 
 us baar maalik ne hamen khaanaa khilaane kii peshkash bhi di
 
 
 " ladki bataati he - "iske baad meri maa ke mata-pita aakar hamen apane saath le gaye, or uske baad se ab tak us parivaar (pita ke parivaar) ko hamane dobaaraa kabhi nahin dekha
 
 
 The father died a few years later, but even then nothing has changed for us regarding that family
 
 
 meri maa or naanaa-nani ne hamaara skool to badla hi, is ummid main hamaare naam bhi badal die ki shaayad isse ham pichhali zindagi bhul saken, or hamaari nai zindagi shuru ho
 
 
 " yaadon main duubati-utaraati yah ladki aage likhti he - "kabhi-kabhi main skool main teacher ko saamne khadaa dekhakar hi ronaa shuru kar detii thi
 
 
 To divert my attention, he was the one who got me enrolled in Bharatanatyam class, and just then, my life changed
 
 
 aath saal kii umr se hi main nrity kar rahi hum
 
 
 "comments iske aage vah bataati he - "meri maa hamen paalane-posane ke liye din-raat kaam karti thi, or bhale hi itane lambey arase tak unhen bandishon main rakhaa gaya tha, unhone hamen kuch bhi padhane-seekhney kii puri azaadi di
 
 
 i have won the Belly Dancing Competition by going to China, and i have been performing all over the country, and my mother has never stopped me
 
 
 " Finally, this young dancer writes - "we have a small world of our own, and we are very happy
" 
 
 itane saal tak ham sangharsh kar paae, isaki iklauti vajah yah rahi ki ham hameshaa, har pal jaanate the ki ek-duusare kaa sahaara banane ke liye ham ek-duusare ke paas hai, or pariwaron ko aisa hi hona bhi chahie
 
 
 So, even though we were not so lucky at first, we were blessed by God that we had a second chance, and we were able to give new meaning to our life

 Posted by Humans of Bombay on tuesday, 15 December 2015"at the age of 7 i saw things that no child that age should see- i had an alcoholic father who would beat my mother up
 
 
 The path to Indian universities has become easier for foreign students who want to come and study in India
 buudhvaar ko maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantralay or videsh mantralay ne milakar study in india (studyinindia
 gov
 in) naam ke kaarykram kii shuruyaat kii
 Through Study in India, it will be easier for foreign students to take admission in 160 premier educational institutions of the country including IIT and IIM
 philhal sarkaar ucch shiksha main 10 se 15% seat videshi chaatro ke liye rakhane kii anumati detii he
 But most of these seats remain vacant as it is difficult for foreign students to complete the admission process by contacting different institutions
 videsh main padhai karne se pehle jaan len ye 7 baaten
 
 
 Through the Applied in India portal, foreign students will be able to go to one place and apply for admission in all these institutions directly and they will get admission in some university according to their qualification
 is kaarykram ko aage badhaane ke liye sarkaar 2 saal main 150 karod rupye kharch karegi taaki uchit shiksha ke kshetra main duniya main bharat kii pahchaan kaayam ho sake
 Let me tell you, about 47000 foreign students study in India
 inamen se zyaadaatar student africa deshon ke alaava afghanistan, nepal, srilanka or bangladesh jaise deshon se aate hai

 pune police ne ek maulavee ko giraftaar kiya he jis par aarope he ki usne ek mahila ko uske pati kii beemaari dur karne ke bahaane bina kapadon ke puja karne ko kaha tha
 It is said that Maulvi had also promised to give three lakh rupees to the woman
 mahila ki maa ne police main shikaayat kar di, jiske baad jaadu-tona kanoon ke tahat maulavee ko giraftaar kar liya gaya
 The police is investigating the case
 pune ke vishrantwari ilaake main rahane vaale aaropee maulavee kaa naam saiyad alam he, peedit mahila ke pati ko tibi kii beemaari he
 Through a woman, she came in contact with the accused maulvi
 aarope he ki maulavee ne mahila kii maa se kaha ki agar tumhaari beti bina kapadon ke ek kamare main puja karegi to pati kii beemaari dur hogi or 3 lakh rupee bhi milenge
 Police is also trying to find out whether this cleric has treated other women as well or if he has some associates
 in dinon swami chinmayanand kaa naam surkhiyon main hai

 maamle kii jaanch esaiti kar rahi he
 But many people do not know who Swami Chinmayananda is? Where did you come from? What were these before? How did he reach the chair of the Minister of State for Home Affairs? Why is the police and administration of UP trying to save them? Who is this Swami who describes himself as close to Chief Minister Yogi Adityanath? And the biggest question is, how did this Baba establish such a huge empire in Shahjahanpur
 shahjahanpur main apana samrajya sthapit karne vaale swami ji asal main upi ke gonda ke rahane vaale hai
 The whole world knows him as Swami Chinmayananda
 magar inkaa asli naam krishnapal singh he
